79996 - Sinister Exotic Filament This Abyssal Filament will pull up to two T1 Cruisers into a pocket of Abyssal Deadspace with an environment saturated with exotic particles that will reduce kinetic resistance but enhance scan resolution.

SOCT scientists have detected a substantial energy surge in this region of Abyssal Deadspace, pointing to a recent large-scale battle. Ongoing activity indicates the presence of several vessels. The SOCT calls upon capsuleers to deploy battle-fitted cruisers and investigate, with the goal of recovering valuable technology and data.

As the conduits are in collapse, space and time around them have become warped to the point of being insulated entirely. As a result, exiting the safe space via one side will appear like entering it from the other.

The pocket is categorized as 'easy' and should be manageable even for those with limited combat experience.

<color=yellow>Warning:</color> Abyssal Deadspace is a particularly harsh and unforgiving environment. After <color=yellow>30 minutes</color> catastrophic collapse of the warp field is predicted, with <color=yellow>destruction of the ship and capsule</color> certain.

Triglavian Origin Conduits will permit the activating ship to return to normal space.		 Abyssal Battlefield Filaments

708483 Capsuleer Day XXI Capsuleer Day XXI
708484 Abyssal Battlefields Abyssal Battlefields
708485 Collapsed conduits to Abyssal Deadspace have been sighted throughout New Eden and Wormhole space. Early investigations reported the presence of Triglavians and Drifters before being destroyed by them. The Society of Conscious Thought has asked capsuleers to pick the investigation by entering these sites and recovering valuable data. Anything else you find is yours to keep.

Explore all regions of space to discover collapsed conduits.

Treacherous Collapsed Conduits are anomalies and will be automatically detected by your ships internal scanner. For these combat sites, the SoCT recommends pilots use cruisers.

Desolate Collapsed Conduits are harder to detect. Uncover these relic sites using scanner probes, and be sure to fit a relic analyzer module so you can access the valuable contents of any containers.

Reports indicate that Collapsed Conduits may contain filament blueprints and rare materials. Once manufactured these filaments will allow you to dive into Abyssal Battlefields. While the New Eden sites are rated as low threat by SOCT, these battlefields are escalating challenges. The deepest Battlegrounds will pose a formidable test even for seasoned veterans.		 Collapsed conduits to Abyssal Deadspace have been sighted throughout New Eden and Wormhole space. Early investigations reported the presence of Triglavians and Drifters before being destroyed by them. The Society of Conscious Thought has asked capsuleers to pick the investigation by entering these sites and recovering valuable data. Anything else you find is yours to keep.

Explore all regions of space to discover collapsed conduits.

Treacherous Collapsed Conduits are anomalies and will be automatically detected by your ships internal scanner. For these combat sites, the SoCT recommends pilots use cruisers.

Desolate Collapsed Conduits are harder to detect. Uncover these relic sites using scanner probes, and be sure to fit a relic analyzer module so you can access the valuable contents of any containers.

Reports indicate that Collapsed Conduits may contain filament blueprints and rare materials. Once manufactured these filaments will allow you to dive into Abyssal Battlefields. While the New Eden sites are rated as low threat by SOCT, these battlefields are escalating challenges. The deepest Battlegrounds will pose a formidable test even for seasoned veterans.

708606 Triglavian Encrypted Conduit Data Triglavian Encrypted Conduit Data Name of item 80873 (Triglavian Data)
708607 This Triglavian data storage device is highly encrypted and loaded with a variety of counter-intrusion programs and defensive security devices that would probably scramble and erase the contents beyond all possibility of retrieval, if not forensically and carefully decrypted and accessed by a specialized facility.

SOCT scientists are keenly interested in the recently collapsed conduits connecting Abyssal Deadspace to New Eden, hinting at a potential reward for any capsuleer delivering this valuable data to their facilities. Both the DED and the Deathless Custodians also exhibit an interest in this matter, offering rewards to capsuleers for providing the data. As the conduits are in collapse, space and time around them have become warped to the point of being insulated entirely. As a result, exiting the safe space via one side will appear like entering it from the other.

The pocket is categorized as 'easy' and should be manageable even for those with limited combat experience.
